If the dislocation is posterior, you must not extend or lift the affected limb off the ground; instead, it should be positioned as if the hip was dislocated backwards, similar to what we've discussed about positioning for double-hip dislocations; they should be on their face with an extended strap as described earlier, and you should press against the joint on a table. It is ready when the patient can extend both legs evenly, at which point you align the thighs and apply the plaster cast along with tight bandages to prevent movement in the hip, resting for 3-4 days before unbinding them and applying more plaster; if they remain even, then rebinding as described earlier for another three days is sufficient. After this period, undo the bindings and allow gentle movement until their limbs regain strength.
de la dislocation dou genoil	Of the dislocation of the knee
Li genous est desaluez selonc III manieres: c’est a savoir, dedens et defuer, et derrier; et ne desalue point devant.	The knees are dislocated in three ways: that is to say, inward and outward, and backward; it does not dislocate forward.
Et li signes si est que tu comande au malaide qu’il plie sa jambe a sa cuixe, et s’ele ne s’aert a sa cuixe, saiches qu’il est desaluez; et li restauration de toutes si est que tu faices seoir le malaide droit, et estende sa jambe s’il puet, et li met ton dos sus sa faice, et met son piet sus tes piez; puis pren son genoil a tes paumes, et retrai entre tes dois, puis plie les II costez dou genoil forment; et uns autres ministres estende son piet, tant que li genous reviegne a son leu, et li signes est qu’il aert bien sa jambe a sa cuixe legierement; et met l’emplastre sus, et fai aerdre la jambe a la cuixe, et les loie ensamble fort III jors ou IIII, puis le deslie; et ne se travaille mie li malaides d’aler, tant que li membres soit confortez.	And the sign of this is that you instruct the patient to bend their leg at the thigh, and if it does not reach the thigh, know that it is dislocated; and the restoration for all these cases is that you make the patient sit upright, and stretch out their leg if they can, and place your back on their face, and put their foot on your feet; then take their knee in your palms, and push between your two hands, then bend the two sides of the knee sharply; and other assistants should stretch their foot until the knee returns to its place, and the sign is that it lightly touches their leg to their thigh; and apply a plaster cast, and make the leg touch the thigh, and bind them together firmly for three or four days, then release it; and do not let the patient walk, until the limb has regained strength.
Et se li membres n’est a point, si aministre estendement fort, si com nos avons dit en la cure de la hainche, tant qu’il soit sanez	And if the limb is not broken, apply strong traction as we have mentioned in the treatment of the hip, until it is healed.
de la dislocation dou talon	Of the dislocation of the heel,
Li talons est aucune fois esmeus, et aucune fois desaluez plenement, et dedens et defuer.	The heels are sometimes bruised, and sometimes completely dislocated, both internally and externally.
Et li signes si est que li cheville est enflee, et tent avant a la partie ou elle est desaluee: li ramenemens si est legier, et le doit on estendre legierement a ses mains quant il est esmeus soulement.	And the sign of this is that the ankle is swollen and more prominent where it is dislocated; the reduction should be gentle, and one must gently extend it with their hands when only bruised.
Et quant il est desaluez dou tot, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide droit, et le tigne I ministres fors par la jambe, desus la cheville; puis trai le piet a toi a ta main destre, et puis a la senestre II fois, puis l’estent en haut, et boute bellement lou piet en haut; et fai ce II fois, si com nos avons dit, em boutant et en traiant lou piet; s’elle revient, c’est bien; se ce non, si rencomence l’ovraige, car il revient; et s’il ne puet revenir ensi, si fai gesir lou malaide sor son dos sus terre, et fiche I passeil fermement en terre entre ses cuixes, et lie drapelz entor, qu’il ne blece lou malaide; puis teigne li ministres la cuixe, et uns autres ministres estende lou piet a ses mains ou a I liien, k’il lie sus le col dou piet; puis estende chescuns ministres igalment, et li passelz soit adés entre les cuixes dou malaide por retenir le malaide quant on l’estent; puis mette li mires igal la dislocation a ses mains, et uns autres ministres teigne la jambe sainne au desoz, et li dislocation revenra hastanment.	And when it is completely dislocated, you should make the patient sit upright and have one minister hold them except for their leg above the ankle; then pull the foot towards yourself with your right hand and then twice with your left hand, then extend upwards and firmly push the foot upwards; do this twice as we have said, pushing and pulling on the foot; if it returns, that is good; but if not, repeat the process because it will return; and if it cannot be returned in this way, then make the patient lie down on their back on the ground, and firmly stick one pole into the earth between their thighs, tying cloth around it so as to avoid hurting the patient; then have one minister hold the thigh while another extends the foot with their hands or a rope tied above the ankle; then extend equally with both ministers, and let the pole be close by between the patient's thighs in order to brace the patient when extending; then place the doctors equally on either side of the dislocation with their hands, and have one other minister hold the healthy leg underneath, and the dislocation will quickly return.
Et quant elle iert a point, si met l’emplastre et estoupes sus, et l’estrain forment, et lie lou piet a la jambe, et warde les ners qui sont sus la cheville derrier, que li liiens ne soit trop estrois; puis le laisse II jors ou III, et se li liiens amolist, si l’estrain; puis le deslie au tier jor ou au quart, et deffent a aler lou malaide par IIII jors; et s’il va devant cel termine, ce n’est mie seurtez qu’il ne desalue encor.	And when it is at the point, place the plaster and swabs on top, apply force, and bind the foot to the leg, securing the nerves above the ankle from behind, ensuring the bindings are not too tight; leave it for two or three days, if the binding loosens, tighten it again; then release the bindings on the third or fourth day, forbidding the patient from walking for four days; if they walk before this period ends, it is not safe as there is a risk of further dislocation.
Et se apostemes chaus i vient, si covient que tu l’apaises, si com nos avons dit autre part, tant qu’il soit sanez.	If pus forms in the abscess, you must soothe it as we have said elsewhere until it is healed.
des dois	twice
Quant li doi sont desaluez, si les covient bellement estendre sens travail, et c’est legiere chose.	When the shoulder is dislocated, it should be gently stretched without strain, which is a simple matter.
Et se li dislocations est en aucun nout dou dos dou piet, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide sus I leu plain ou sus .ie. table tot droit, et met ton piet sus ce qui apert de ces jointures, puis presse a ton piet forment, tant qu’il reviegne; et quant il est igalz, et il n’i apert nient, si met desoz la plante dou piet une table a II chiés, puis l’estrain forment, et le laisse III jors, puis le deslie; et le fai reposer, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if the dislocation is in any nut of your back from your foot, you must make the patient sit on a flat surface or on a straight table, and place your foot on what appears to be these joints, then press hard with your foot until it returns; when it is equalized, and nothing seems wrong, put under the sole of the foot a two-legged table, then strain it strongly, and leave it three days, then release it; and let him rest until he is healed.
de plaie et de dislocation ensamble	For wounds and dislocations together, you must first prepare the cautery of fire and use coals or stones to burn them red-hot; then take wax, pitch, rosin, fat, and oil, mixing all five substances. Take two small pieces of cloth, rub them with hog lard, spread the mixture on one side, and place it where you see that there is a dislocation. Let him rest for some time until the swelling goes down; then take some fine linen, soak it in water, and bind around his limb from the head to the foot of the member. Leave it bound tightly and let him sit still like this until the wound heals completely, or nearly so, if necessary.
Quant plaie vient avec la dislocation, et on la vuet restorer, maintes fois avient que li malaides muert: si ne soies mie presumptuous en la cure, se tu n’es saiges en l’art et tu ne l’as useit longement, et se tu n’es pitous et misericors et tardis, ne mie hardis; et use au comencement de choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et laisse le malaide en la main Deu, se tu n’i vois esperance de santeit; et quant tu i vois esperance, si ramoinne maintenant le membre au leu, ainsois que li apostemes chaus i viegne; et quant li membres est a leu, si aministre choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et cure la plaie, si com il covient, d’oignemens desiccatis; et se avec la dislocation a brisure, et os menus desevrez, si les oste, et fai ce que nos avons dit en maladies simples; et te garde d’entrer en voie de paour, selonc ce que j’ai dit, car ce te vaut mues selonc ton Creator, et por la saveteit de t’arme et de ton cors.	When a wound comes with dislocation and one wants to restore it, often the patient dies: so do not be presumptuous in treatment if you are not wise in this art or experienced, nor tardy, nor uncompassionate; first use cooling remedies for the abscess, leaving the patient in God's hands if you see no hope of health; but when you have seen a chance at recovery, move the limb back into place now before any hot abscesses appear and develop it; and once the limb is back where it should be then give him warm soothing things to treat the swelling of his wounds and cure the wound with drying ointments. If there are broken bits of bone left in the joint that dislocation has knocked apart, remove them and do as we have said for simple diseases. Be mindful always of fear, which I have mentioned; because it is important how you proceed according to your creator's design, preserving both your soul and body.
